Materials with optical properties at reference wavelength 380 nm.

Data format:
(1) Material name
(2) Concentration/occupied volume/amount (type*)
(3) Optical depth (4) Single-scattering albedo (5) Asymmetry factor
(6) Absorption optical depth     (7) Scattering optical depth
(8) Absorption coefficient [1/m] (9) Scattering coefficient [1/m]
(10) Delta-fit scattering scaling factor
* sf = scaling factor, vf = volume fraction
